                                    ending of the chapter is: uttaratantre śoṣacikitsā
                                    aṣṭatriṃsattamaḥ kāyacikitsāyāṃ tṛtīyodhyāyaḥ || So it
                                    looks like it is being called chapter 38, not 41. </note>

                                <note resp="Vandana Lele">
                                    <list>
                                        <item>1) I have doubt about the chapter number as
                                            the colophon of the manuscript mentions:
                                            "uttaratantre'ṣṭapañcāśattamaḥ kāyacikitsāyāṃ
                                            yonivyāpaccikitsā trayoviṅśatitamo'dhyāyaḥ
                                            samāptaḥ ||" As I have understood it, the
                                            above heading is given to the subject of this
                                            mail . I have also marked the same in the
                                            transcription file. Please comment.</item>
                                        <item>2) The folios which I have transcribed i.e
                                            480r:3, 480v, 481r, 481v are not
                                            paginated.</item>
                                        <item>3) Missing verses: 6.38.2, 3, 4, 5ab, 5cd,
                                            5, 6, 7, 6.38.30ab, 32cd, 32ef Probably,
                                            6.38.4.1 is left out to mark in the vulgate
                                            copy, like other verses 6.38.3.1, 6.38.2 etc.
                                            which are in manuscript. I am not sure about
                                            this observation. In vulgate, verse number
                                            6.38.8.1 is shown as missing but in manuscript
                                            I could not find different text relating to
                                            that for addition. (Here, also I may be
                                            wrong.)</item>
                                        <item>4) Additions: 6.38.3.1, 3.2, 4.1, 5.1, 6.1,
                                            7.1</item>
                                        <item>5) SS. 6.38.8cd, 17 cd , 23cd, 26cd, 27cd -
                                            the second half has different text.</item>
                                        <item>6) SS.6.38.28 ab - the first half has
                                            different text.</item>
                                    </list>
                                </note>
                                <note resp="Vandana Lele"> This adhyaya is numbered 47 in
                                    the vulgate and 44.9 in NAK 5-333 <list>

                                             me is intermingled with 6.47.4cd which is
                                             shown missing by me.</item>
                                             <item>ii) 6.47.20cd - the second half verse

                                             has different text. </item>

                                             whereas 44ab has rest of the text.</item>

                                             folios are not noted by me in the
